I think they were inundated with tourist for CNY, so I can't really fault them for that. Everytime I went down, the lobby was always crowded with people in line. Normally the manager/host has some friendly banter, but they were too busy.

Housekeeping as always was wonderful!

Had the buffet dinner on my birthday. The price was seemingly much more expensive than normal. They also only gave 1/2 lobster. Other hotel buffets don't limit the number as long as you eat them. The selection of food also seemed more limited than what it was last time I was there (or maybe just seemed that way due to the price). So the food was good, but not the value.

After 4 days there, I asked for a late check out.  I was just simply told 'no'. I know it's a courtesy of the hotel to do, but it's the first time there which I didn't get one and where I just got a straight no. No reason, not asking what time, or anything. Once again, I know they are probably extra busy with CNY travelers.

Anyway, I'll still go back. Like I said, the service was less than stellar, but still overall good. Though I may skip the buffet dinner next time.

The good:

- The view from the pricier river-view room was nice.

- Breakfast was fine, but with limited choices

The bad:

- Taxis are not allowed to drive to the hotel entrance and no staff available to help. Had to carry our suitcases from the curb into the lobby by ourselves.

- Swimming pool and gym were closed, citing "pandemic control requirements", which seem to be the excuse for everything that is not handled professionally at this hotel. The hotel said that this would have been stated on trip.com (which it wasn't at the time of booking and checking in) and trip.com stated that they were not responsible for solving such issue, since the fees were paid to the hotel directly.

- The rooms are old and lack the basic facilities which one would expect from a 5-star hotel such as a coffee maker - instead only instant coffee is offered. Also, noise from the hall and neighboring rooms could be heard during the night.

- Staff at the entrance were inefficient and rude when checking health codes upon each return to the hotel.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Grand Executive River-view Suite
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:4.5
posted:Posted May 3, 2024
msg:Overall, I am satisfied.
Advantages: 1. The package includes: room upgrades depending on room availability, and the Diplomat Suite is upgraded for holidays, which is larger than the original suite.
2. The Diplomat Suite has a smart toilet, electric curtains, coffee machine, Bluetooth speakers, etc. The Bluetooth sound effect is great.
3. There is a TV in the living room and the TV in the room can play normally.
4. The kettle, hair dryer, iron and other equipment in the room can be used normally. (I didn't move them and brought them myself)
4. The bathroom is very large, with a double wash basin, makeup mirror, bathtub, shower room, smart toilet (separate, also in the bathroom), and another smart toilet (smart toilet, wash basin with mirror).
5. The entire suite is very large and comfortable.
6. There is an independent cloakroom, with 2 sets of irons, ironing boards, and shoe horns.
7. The bedroom has an independent door, and there are TVs, Bluetooth speakers, coffee tables, sofa stools, small reading tables and stools + reading lamps in the bedroom.
8. There is a separate tea room, equipped with a refrigerator, coffee machine, tea set, tea bags and capsule coffee.
9. The bathroom is equipped with Guerlain toiletries
10. In addition, the service attitude was good when dining at the VIP Club on the 83rd floor (the package also included breakfast on the 54th floor, but I didn't go).
Disadvantages:
1. The suite I booked said that there was a private butler for check-in, but I still had to queue up to check in. When it was my turn to check in, I was asked if I needed to sit upstairs to check in. If I was in line, did I still have to go upstairs to go through the process again?
2. The receptionist stood there smiling and polite, but he also brought children and gave gifts to the little girls of other guests (the room he stayed in was 2588 a night, and he was not short of gifts). We took the initiative to ask "Do I need to queue up to check in?" He didn't even say to sit down.
3. The room facilities are the same as those mentioned in the bad reviews. The air conditioner made a sound all night and the smart toilet splashed chrysanthemums.
4. There is a white bag similar to desiccant in the wash basin in the tea room, with "throw away" written on it
5. Living on the 84th floor, you need to take the elevator twice to the 1st floor to get takeout.
6. There is no guide for placing items in the room, and the hair dryer and slippers are hidden relatively secretly.
7. There is no room service reminder (such as what services can be enjoyed when checking in the room, etc.). The hardware of a 5-star hotel is OK, but the personal experience of soft services needs to be strengthened.

msg:It should be said that I have a special fate with Jinmao Grand Hyatt because my wedding was held here, so this time I returned to celebrate my second anniversary. Let‚Äôs talk about the experience of staying:
1. Geographical location. Excellent, Jinmao Grand Hyatt is located in the upper half of Jinmao Tower, with excellent views, especially the Diplomat Suite we stayed in this time, which has a 180-degree panoramic view, overlooking the entire Century Avenue extending from the Huangpu River to the east.
2. Hotel facilities. Because the hotel has been open for more than 20 years, the decoration of the facilities has a certain sense of age. It can be seen that it was a top-notch work at the turn of the century. The hotel rooms are a fusion of modern style and Chinese culture, and are generally well maintained. .
3. Catering facilities: The hotel is fully equipped with restaurants of various grades including buffet, Chinese food, Western food, and bar. Yin Art Restaurant has a great environment but is expensive. The buffet restaurant for breakfast is large and has a very good view. The breakfast is divided into Chinese and Western areas and is very rich.
4. Executive Lounge: Guests who enjoy the privileges of the Club Club can also go to the Club Club on the 83rd floor to enjoy breakfast, all-day refreshments, snacks and evening drinks. However, the breakfast varieties in the Club Club are relatively small, and the afternoon tea snacks are among the same five-star hotels in Shanghai. The executive lounge of a first-class hotel is also slightly lacking, but the waiters and ladies at the VIP Club are all beautiful and enthusiastic, and the service experience is pretty good.
5. Recreation and sports facilities: The hotel gym has a good environment and a good view. The fitness equipment is complete and well maintained. The swimming pool is beautiful but relatively small and needs to be booked in advance.
6. Overall service: As an old five-star hotel, the service quality is generally commendable. The staff are very enthusiastic and professional. The concierge will take the initiative to help transport large luggage to the guest room. Guests staying in the hotel can also use the underground garage. Free parking.

msg:Since the epidemic, I have really played Shanghai all over. On the eve of Valentine's Day, I specially chose the Grand Hyatt Hotel in Jin Mao Tower, one of the four-piece suites in the center of Lujiazui, to stay for one night to experience the height and beautiful night view of Shanghai.
üöó Transportation: The hotel is located in the central area of Lujiazui. You can get there by self-driving from the Yan'an East Road Tunnel and turn two turns. Hotel guests need to park their car in the underground parking garage of Jinmao Building, and go out to the concierge on the first floor to report the room number and license plate That's it.
üçÉ Environment:
It has been almost 24 years since the hotel opened, and it has been renovated once in 14 years, but it has been well maintained so far. It can be seen that the management of the hyatt group is in place. The hotel environment is very good, belonging to high-end positioning. The room is ok except that the room is a bit stuffy and the bed is not big enough.
üßπHygiene:
The room is very clean, and the public areas are also well-organized. Although the hotel is very large, there are service staff everywhere.
üîîService:
The first time I stayed in a hotel, there was a "white coat" for epidemic monitoring and security dog inspection, and I felt very relieved. There are a lot of people for breakfast, and we need to queue up to enter the venue. The supplement is very timely. This time, I also received a panoramic view table, which is very happy.
In general, the price of about 1,000 yuan to live in the Grand Hyatt Lujiazui feels very worthwhile, and I will have the opportunity to brush it again in the future.

Although it is not the best viewing position, the scenery is still good. Although the room is traditional Chinese style, it is relatively ordinary but very clean. The grade of furniture materials is good. There is a bathtub and a shower, and the shower is the kind of combination that can be adjusted according to your needs. The window of the room cannot be opened, so it is hot when there is sunshine. In this season, it seems that the hotel does not have air-conditioning. It will be hot after staying in the room for a long time, which will affect sleep at night. Maybe it will improve after turning on the air-conditioning. . The buffet in the hotel is relatively rich, Chinese and Western styles are distributed on the left and right sides. There are many varieties and quality, especially fruits, such as red heart pomelo, yellow orange, passion fruit, star fruit and so on. The swimming pool of the hotel is not big on the 57th floor. The two swimming lanes are only about ten meters in length. The water is not very clear. There are many children on weekends, but there is a hot spring pool to soak in. The western restaurant on the 87th floor of the hotel has a good night view. The dishes are okay, but the quantity is a little smaller. It would be better if it was arranged on the side of the Oriental Pearl. All in all, the experience of staying at the Grand Hyatt was very pleasant.
